# Gap Tasks — implementation specs

> One pick-up-cold task per open gap: context, problem (with file:line), steps, files,
> a Definition-of-Done **contract**, the verification command, dependencies, and pitfalls.
> Generated 2026-06-24 from the `gap-task-specs` workflow (each spec authored by an agent
> that read the cited source files). Severities use the fast-track scheme from `docs/index.html`:
> **URGENT [!]** blocks the fast track to Spark + report start · **HIGH** needed for a full
> report · **MID** should-have · **LOW** nice-to-have. Gap evidence/closure rows: `docs/GAP_REGISTER.md`.
> Wave ordering & contracts: `docs/TASKS.md`.

Hard rules every task must respect: raw Bronze stays immutable; numeric stat merges stay
deterministic (no LLM rewriting numbers); runtime outputs go under `output/`; never fabricate
data; tests must not depend on `coursework/` data (use `tmp_path`/fixtures).



## URGENT [!]

### GAP-009 — Spark evidence job: read real Gold Parquet, write coverage evidence (Spark version, row/col counts, files written)

`URGENT [!]` · level **spark** · effort **M** · depends on: GAP-017 (pin `pyspark==4.1.*` + `delta-spark==4.1.*`, document S3A Maven packages `org.apache.hadoop:hadoop-aws:3.4.1,software.amazon.awssdk:bundle:2.24.6`, and require JDK 17 or 21) — must be resolved in the same change or a prior Wave-1 PR; installing unbounded pyspark is not allowed., A real Gold Parquet to read — already satisfied by `gold/first-real-result` (output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/railway_ml.parquet, 2968x4). GAP-007 (Gold-from-persisted-Silver) is a bonus, NOT a blocker., JDK 17 or 21 install + JAVA_HOME (and, on native Windows, winutils.exe/hadoop.dll per STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:206-210) are environment prerequisites to actually RUN Spark; the import/pin guard test does not need them.

**Build:** Create the importable PySpark entrypoint `railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage` that reads a real Gold Parquet with a SparkSession and writes a coverage-evidence manifest plus a Spark-written output Parquet directory under `output/evidence/spark/`, recording Spark version, input/output row+column counts, files/partitions written, and duration.

**Context.** This is THE graded deliverable for the course (`docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:25,145-150`, `docs/index.html:351` "The graded target."). The pipeline reads `web sources → Bronze → Silver → Gold → (Spark) → report`; today the train is at Gold and Spark is the next stop. GAP-009 sits on the critical path between `gold/first-real-result` (done, real Gold exists) and `report/draft` (GAP-011, blocked until Spark evidence exists). It is Wave 2 in `docs/TASKS.md:129-136` (Contract B) and depends on the GAP-017 dependency pin. Closing it produces the first artifact a Spark grade and the report can cite.

**Problem.** No Spark code exists anywhere in the repo. `src/railway_lakehouse/` has bronze/silver/gold packages but NO `spark_jobs/` package (verified: `find src -type d -name "spark*"` returns nothing), so the registered verification command `python -m railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage` fails at import (`ModuleNotFoundError`). Two blocking environment facts confirmed locally: (1) `pyspark` is NOT installed (`python -c "import pyspark"` -> ModuleNotFoundError); (2) only Java 8 is present (`java -version` -> `1.8.0_491`). GAP-017 resolves the old unbounded Spark extra by pinning the Python packages to Spark 4.1-compatible lines and moving S3A to Maven coordinates instead of pip. Separately, the GAP-009 registered command's input path `output/evidence/live/railway_ml.parquet` DOES NOT EXIST (`output/evidence/live/` is absent). The real Gold Parquet files that DO exist are: `output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/railway_ml.parquet` (2968 rows × 4 cols: geo, year, rail_freight_tonne_km, rail_network_length_km — the richest real Gold), `output/evidence/first-real-gold-local-stats-v2/railway_ml.parquet` (2139×3), and `output/evidence/fixture-e2e/railway_ml.parquet` (4×3). If the job blindly trusts a missing `--input` it will either crash opaquely or (the GAP-012-class trap) silently process nothing — the job must fail loudly on a missing/empty input.

**Steps.**
1. RESEARCH (mandatory per coursework workflow): invoke the `research-orchestrator` skill; route PySpark API questions through Context7 or Ref (SparkSession.builder, DataFrame.read.parquet, count/columns, write.parquet directory semantics, spark.version). Write the research record to `.planning/coursework/research/bigdata/spark-evidence-job.md` naming research-orchestrator, the routed provider(s), queries, and source URLs (e.g. https://spark.apache.org/docs/latest/sql-data-sources-parquet.html). Cross-check the version stack against `docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:188-216`.
2. DEPENDENCY (GAP-017) — pin the Spark stack before installing. In `pyproject.toml:26-28`, the `spark` extra must contain only resolvable Python packages: `pyspark==4.1.*` and `delta-spark==4.1.*`. S3A is not a pip dependency; use the shared `railway_lakehouse.spark_config.SPARK_S3A_PACKAGES` value (`org.apache.hadoop:hadoop-aws:3.4.1,software.amazon.awssdk:bundle:2.24.6`) if a later job needs `spark.jars.packages`. Record JDK 17 or 21 in README/manifest. Do this in the same change OR confirm a prior Wave-1 PR already pinned it; do not install an unbounded pyspark.
3. Create the package directory `src/railway_lakehouse/spark_jobs/` with `__init__.py` (docstring only, no logic).
4. Create `src/railway_lakehouse/spark_jobs/coverage.py` exposing pure, importable functions plus a `main(argv=None)` CLI. Argparse args mirroring the registered command and the existing pipeline idiom (`pipeline.py:45-78`): `--input` (default to a REAL existing Gold parquet — use `output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/railway_ml.parquet`, the 2968×4 richest real Gold — NOT the nonexistent `output/evidence/live/...`), `--out` (default `output/evidence/spark/`), and `--master` (default `local[*]`).
5. Implement a `build_session(master)` helper using `SparkSession.builder.appName('railway-coverage').master(master).getOrCreate()`. Keep it minimal: reading plain local Parquet needs no extra JARs (per `STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:201-203`). Do NOT add `s3a`/hadoop-aws config in this job — the registered command reads a local `file://` Gold parquet; MinIO/s3a is explicitly out of scope here and is a later GAP-010/GAP-013 follow-up.
6. Implement `run_coverage(spark, input_path, out_dir) -> dict`: (a) validate the input — if `Path(input_path)` does not exist, raise `FileNotFoundError` with the path and a hint ('run the Gold pipeline first or pass --input to an existing Gold parquet'); (b) read with `spark.read.parquet(input_path)`; (c) capture `in_rows = df.count()`, `in_cols = len(df.columns)`, `columns = df.columns`; (d) FAIL LOUDLY if `in_rows == 0` (raise ValueError — closes the GAP-012-class silent-empty trap, mirroring the GAP-012 closure intent); (e) compute a small deterministic Spark aggregation that demonstrates real distributed processing on the real schema, e.g. per-`geo` non-null coverage counts and per-`year` row counts using `groupBy(...).count()` / `agg(F.count(...))` so the job does genuine Spark work, not just a passthrough; (f) write the aggregation out via `out_df.write.mode('overwrite').parquet(<out_dir>/coverage_by_geo_year)` — note PySpark writes a DIRECTORY of part-files + `_SUCCESS`, not a single .parquet file (`STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:203`); (g) capture `out_rows`, `out_cols`, and the list of files/partitions written by scanning the output directory.
7. Write the evidence manifest, mirroring the established `scripts/minio_smoke.py` manifest idiom (UTC start/finish ISO timestamps, status, evidence_path) and the `write_gold_counts` shape (`pipeline.py:146-175`). Manifest at `output/evidence/spark/manifest.json` must contain at minimum (per `docs/VERIFICATION.md:175-185`): `command`, `spark_version` (from `spark.version`), `input_path`, `input_rows`, `input_columns`, `input_column_names`, `output_path`, `output_rows`, `output_columns`, `files_written` (the part-file list incl. `_SUCCESS`), `partitions_written`, `duration_seconds`, `status` ('passed'/'failed'), and timestamps. Write via a small `_write_json` helper (mkdir parents) exactly like `scripts/minio_smoke.py:56-58`. Always call `spark.stop()` in a finally block.
8. Wrap `main()` so an exception writes a `status:'failed'` manifest with the error and a hint (mirror `scripts/minio_smoke.py:121-136`) and returns a nonzero exit code; success prints the evidence path and returns 0. Keep `if __name__ == '__main__': sys.exit(main())`.
9. Add a deterministic test file `tests/test_spark_coverage.py`. Set `pytestmark = pytest.mark.spark` (the marker already exists in `pyproject.toml:46` but currently selects 0 tests). At module top, `pyspark = pytest.importorskip('pyspark')` so the test SKIPS cleanly when pyspark is absent (it is not installed in the default `[test]` env, so `pytest -q` stays green). The test must NOT depend on `coursework/`/`output/` data: build a tiny Gold parquet in `tmp_path` with pandas (a few geo/year/feature rows), run `coverage.run_coverage(...)`/`coverage.main([...])` in `local[1]` master, then assert: input_rows/input_columns are correct, the output parquet directory + `_SUCCESS` exist, manifest.json exists with a non-empty `spark_version` and matching counts, and that a MISSING `--input` raises `FileNotFoundError` and a 0-row input raises `ValueError` (deterministic guard, no network/Docker).
10. Add an import/config guard unit test (runs WITHOUT pyspark, marker `unit`) — e.g. extend an existing test or add to the new file a separately-markered function — asserting `import railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage` succeeds, that `coverage.main` and `coverage.run_coverage` are callable, and that the `spark` extra in pyproject pins pyspark to `4.1.*` while S3A is represented by `spark.jars.packages` Maven coordinates (string check, mirroring `tests/test_infra_minio.py:32-40`). This proves GAP-009's import contract + GAP-017 pin deterministically in CI even on Java 8 / no-pyspark machines. Keep pyspark-dependent assertions out of this unit test.
11. DOCS / DASHBOARD SYNC (Hard Rule, `AGENTS.md:81`): update `docs/VERIFICATION.md` (replace the placeholder 'Spark Evidence' future section at lines 175-185 with the real command + observed results once run), add the Spark command to `README.md`, flip `docs/TASKS.md:86` `spark/evidence-job` status from `todo` to `done` (with the real evidence shape), and update the matching chip/metric in `docs/index.html:351,393`. Set GAP-009 status in `docs/GAP_REGISTER.md:25` to `in_progress`/`closed` and append a row to the Test Failure Mapping table. Append a handoff entry to `docs/PROGRESS_LOG.md` using the AGENTS.md template.
12. RUN + RECORD EVIDENCE: with the pinned PySpark 4.1.x installed and `JAVA_HOME` on JDK 17 or 21, run the registered command but with a REAL input (the nonexistent default path is the trap): `python -m railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage --input output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/railway_ml.parquet --out output/evidence/spark/`. Commit `output/evidence/spark/manifest.json` and the output parquet directory (note `.gitignore:27` ignores only `output/evidence/**/bronze/`, NOT `output/evidence/spark/`, so spark evidence IS committable; `spark-warehouse/` is gitignored at line 32).

**Files to touch:** `src/railway_lakehouse/spark_jobs/__init__.py (new)`  `src/railway_lakehouse/spark_jobs/coverage.py (new)`  `tests/test_spark_coverage.py (new)`  `pyproject.toml (confirm spark extra pins PySpark 4.1.x + delta-spark 4.1.x; GAP-017)`  `src/railway_lakehouse/spark_config.py (consume S3A Maven package constants if needed)`  `docs/VERIFICATION.md (replace placeholder Spark Evidence section with real command + results)`  `README.md (add Spark command + JDK note)`  `docs/TASKS.md (spark/evidence-job todo -> done)`  `docs/GAP_REGISTER.md (GAP-009 status + Test Failure Mapping row)`  `docs/index.html (spark chip/metric)`  `docs/PROGRESS_LOG.md (handoff entry)`  `.planning/coursework/research/bigdata/spark-evidence-job.md (research record, new)`

**Definition of Done (contract).**
- [ ] `python -c "import railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage"` succeeds (the registered module path imports — closes the core GAP-009 import gap).
- [ ] `python -m railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage --input output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/railway_ml.parquet --out output/evidence/spark/` exits 0 and writes `output/evidence/spark/manifest.json` plus a Spark output parquet directory (part-files + `_SUCCESS`).
- [ ] The committed `output/evidence/spark/manifest.json` records: spark_version (non-empty), input_path, input_rows (=2968 for the inventory-live Gold) and input_columns (=4), output_rows/output_columns, files_written + partitions_written, duration_seconds, status='passed', and UTC timestamps — every field `docs/VERIFICATION.md:177-185` asks for.
- [ ] Input validation: a missing `--input` raises `FileNotFoundError` with the path + a remediation hint; a 0-row input raises `ValueError` (no silent-empty output — closes the GAP-012-class trap).
- [ ] `pyproject.toml` `spark` extra pins `pyspark==4.1.*` and `delta-spark==4.1.*` only; `pip install --dry-run '.[spark]'` resolves PySpark 4.1.x, and S3A is supplied through Spark Maven packages `org.apache.hadoop:hadoop-aws:3.4.1,software.amazon.awssdk:bundle:2.24.6` when needed; JDK 17 or 21 recorded in README/manifest.
- [ ] Deterministic test `tests/test_spark_coverage.py` exists: the `spark`-markered test builds its Gold input in `tmp_path` (no `coursework/`/`output/` dependency) and is collected when pyspark is present; the `unit`-markered import/pin guard passes with NO pyspark installed.
- [ ] `python -m pytest -q` stays green on the default `[test]` env (pyspark-dependent test SKIPS via `importorskip`; no new failures, no xfail).
- [ ] Dashboard + docs synced in the same change (Hard Rule, AGENTS.md:81): `docs/TASKS.md` spark/evidence-job = done, `docs/index.html` chip updated, `docs/GAP_REGISTER.md` GAP-009 status updated + Test Failure Mapping row added, `docs/VERIFICATION.md` real Spark section, `docs/PROGRESS_LOG.md` handoff entry.
- [ ] Raw Bronze untouched; numeric Gold values are read verbatim into Spark and aggregated deterministically with no LLM involvement; all outputs are under `output/evidence/spark/`.
- [ ] Research record written at `.planning/coursework/research/bigdata/spark-evidence-job.md` naming research-orchestrator + routed MCP provider(s) + source URLs.

**Verify:** `Primary (deterministic, CI-safe, no Spark needed): `python -m pytest -q -m "unit or integration"` (stays green; import/pin guard passes) AND `python -c "import railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage"`. With pinned PySpark 4.1.x + JDK 17 or 21 installed: `python -m pytest -q -m spark` (spark test passes) AND the registered evidence command with a REAL input: `python -m railway_lakehouse.spark_jobs.coverage --input output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/railway_ml.parquet --out output/evidence/spark/` then `python -m json.tool output/evidence/spark/manifest.json`. Note: the GAP-register's literal command uses `--input output/evidence/live/railway_ml.parquet`, which does NOT exist on disk — point `--input` at a real Gold parquet (inventory-live-2026-06-23) or generate `output/evidence/live/` first via a live pipeline run.`

**Pitfalls.** "DO NOT trust the GAP-register's literal `--input output/evidence/live/railway_ml.parquet` — that path does not exist; default and document a real Gold (inventory-live-2026-06-23). DO NOT silently process a missing/empty input (the GAP-012 anti-pattern) — fail loudly. Hard Rules (AGENTS.md:74-81): raw Bronze stays immutable (this job only READS Gold); numeric values are read verbatim and aggregated deterministically — NO LLM rewriting of numbers; all outputs under output/ (here output/evidence/spark/). PySpark writes a DIRECTORY of part-files + `_SUCCESS`, not a single .parquet file — count/list files accordingly. Keep pyspark OUT of the default `[test]` install so `pytest -q` stays green; gate the spark test with `pytest.importorskip('pyspark')` and the `spark` marker (already registered, pyproject.toml:46). The Spark extra is pinned to the Python packages only; do not add JVM artifacts as fake pip dependencies. Always `spark.stop()` in finally to avoid lingering JVMs. Tests must build inputs in tmp_path, never read coursework/ or output/ data (AGENTS.md / CLAUDE.md testing rule). `output/evidence/spark/` is NOT gitignored (only `output/evidence/**/bronze/` and `spark-warehouse/` are) so the manifest + output parquet are committable evidence. Dashboard sync (docs/TASKS.md + docs/index.html) is part of DoD, not optional. Do not add s3a/MinIO config to this job — local file:// Parquet only; s3a is a later follow-up that should consume `railway_lakehouse.spark_config.SPARK_S3A_PACKAGES`."

### GAP-011 — Author the evidence-grounded report + presentation drafts under output/, with a deterministic evidence-link checker test

`URGENT [!]` · level **report** · effort **M** · depends on: GAP-009 (Spark evidence job) — soft dependency: required only to fill the report's Spark RESULTS section; the rest of the report (and this task's Definition of Done) does not block on it. The Spark section ships as a marked placeholder until GAP-009 lands, then is updated from output/evidence/spark/., Already-satisfied inputs (no work needed): GAP-010 live World Bank Gold + MinIO smoke evidence and GAP-004 fixture evidence already exist and are git-tracked under output/evidence/.

**Build:** Create output/report/ and output/presentation/ Markdown drafts in which every quantitative data claim cites a committed evidence artifact under output/evidence/, and add a deterministic test that fails if any cited evidence path is missing or any headline number drifts from the evidence JSON.

**Context.** GAP-011 is the final S5 deliverable: the course report and presentation. It sits at the very end of the data spine (Bronze → Silver → Gold → Spark → report) and is currently "not started beyond organization notes" (GAP_REGISTER.md:27; STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:26). The closure criterion is "Drafts link every data claim to evidence artifacts" verified by "Manual review of output/report/ and output/presentation/" (GAP_REGISTER.md:27). The grading rubric rewards web data gathering, automatic updates, a Big Data engine, analysis, and a report/presentation — so the report must honestly narrate what is proven (real World Bank Bronze→Silver→Gold; local MinIO object storage) and what is not yet (live-MinIO WB stats path GAP-013, Eurostat→Gold mapping GAP-013/023, Ollama/news GAP-006, Spark GAP-009). This task is gated behind the Spark evidence job in the roadmap (TASKS.md:138-139), but the report scaffold + all already-proven claims can and should be drafted now; the Spark section stays a clearly-marked placeholder until GAP-009 lands.

**Problem.** No report or presentation deliverable exists. `output/report/` and `output/presentation/` directories are absent (confirmed: `find output -maxdepth 3 -type d` lists only `output/evidence`, `output/project-organization`, `output/runtime`; `git ls-files output/report output/presentation` returns nothing). `docs/VERIFICATION.md:187-199` already prescribes this exact layout (`output/{evidence,runtime,report,presentation}`) but nothing fills it. The only report-shaped file, `output/project-organization/REPORT.md`, is a 2026-06-21 organization note about scaffolding (lines 1-12), not a data report, and cites no evidence artifacts. There is no mechanism — manual or automated — ensuring a future report's numbers match the committed evidence JSON, so the closure criterion ("every data claim links to evidence") is unenforceable today. The authoritative numbers a report must cite already exist and are git-tracked: `output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/counts.json` (2968 rows × 4 cols, geos 151, AT/HU present, years 1995–2021, at_rows/hu_rows=27), its `manifest.json` (World Bank passed: 3 artifacts, 17,065,815 bytes, sha256 per artifact; Eurostat failed on RemoteDisconnected), `inventory_samples.json` (concrete AT/HU yearly values, e.g. AT 1995 freight=13715, network=5672; silver_stats reloaded_rows=35112), `output/evidence/first-real-gold-local-stats-v2/counts.json` (the earlier 2139×3 single-feature smoke), and `output/evidence/minio-smoke/manifest.json` (roundtrip_ok=true, buckets bronze/silver/gold, 32 B). These numbers are produced deterministically by `pipeline.py:146-175` `write_gold_counts` and `gold/build.py` (no LLM touches numbers — `gold/build.py:13` "Two deterministic stages, no LLM").

**Steps.**
1. Read the canonical evidence the report will cite so every number is copied, not invented: output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/{counts.json,manifest.json,inventory_samples.json,crosswalk_cache.json}, output/evidence/first-real-gold-local-stats-v2/counts.json, output/evidence/minio-smoke/manifest.json, and the Bronze live-check manifests under output/evidence/{ksh-live-check-2026-06-22-current,uic-live-check-2026-06-22,worldbank-live-check-2026-06-22,rss-feed-health-2026-06-22,statistik-austria-live-check-2026-06-22}/manifest.json. Treat the *.json values as the single source of truth for every figure in the report.
2. Create output/report/REPORT.md. Structure it as: (1) Problem & dataset (HU/AT rail statistics + news; sources table mirroring STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:64-73 Data Inventory); (2) Architecture (Bronze→Silver→Gold→Spark→report; lakehouse with MinIO object storage; cite docs/ARCHITECTURE.md and docs/DATA_CONTRACTS.md); (3) What is proven end-to-end TODAY — the live World Bank Bronze→Silver→Gold run: 2,968 rows × 4 columns [geo, year, rail_freight_tonne_km, rail_network_length_km], 151 geos, 1995–2021, AT/HU 27 rows each, with the concrete sample values AT 1995 freight=13715 network=5672 and HU 1995 freight=8337 network=7988 — each figure followed by an inline citation to its evidence file (counts.json / inventory_samples.json); (4) Object storage: local MinIO proven via scripts/minio_smoke.py (roundtrip_ok=true, bronze/silver/gold buckets) citing minio-smoke/manifest.json; (5) Bronze source coverage table citing each source's live-check manifest (KSH 6 XLSX/92,509 B; UIC 2 PDF/2,109,240 B; World Bank 3 artifacts/17,065,815 B; etc.); (6) an explicit, honest 'Known gaps / not yet proven' section listing GAP-013 (live-MinIO stats path drops World Bank — the headline Gold used --bronze-root, not the live MinIO read path), Eurostat reaches Silver but not Gold (SDMX header / unmapped, GAP-013/GAP-023), Ollama/news extraction unrun (GAP-006), and Spark not yet built (GAP-009) — link each to its GAP_REGISTER.md row; (7) a Spark results placeholder clearly marked '[PENDING GAP-009 — to be filled from output/evidence/spark/ once the Spark job runs]'.
3. Add an 'Evidence index' section at the end of REPORT.md: a Markdown table mapping each headline claim → exact evidence path → the JSON key/value that backs it (e.g. 'Gold rows = 2968 | output/evidence/inventory-live-2026-06-23/counts.json | rows=2968'). This table is both human-auditable and the anchor the checker test parses.
4. Create output/presentation/PRESENTATION.md as a slide-deck-style outline (one '## Slide N' per slide, speaker notes as blockquotes). Slides: title; problem; architecture diagram description; data sources; the proven 2,968×4 Gold result with the AT/HU sample numbers; MinIO storage; Spark plan/results-placeholder; honest gaps; conclusion/next steps. Every numeric slide reuses the SAME figures and the SAME evidence citations as REPORT.md (no new or rounded numbers).
5. Author tests/test_report_evidence_links.py marked @pytest.mark.unit. The test must: (a) assert output/report/REPORT.md and output/presentation/PRESENTATION.md exist; (b) extract every `output/evidence/...` path mentioned in both files (regex) and assert each path exists on disk relative to the repo root; (c) for a small curated set of headline numbers, load the backing evidence JSON (e.g. json.load(counts.json)) and assert the integer/string appears verbatim in REPORT.md text — proving the prose matches the artifact and catching numeric drift. Do NOT hardcode the numbers as literals duplicated from the doc; read them from the evidence JSON so the test stays a real cross-check. The test reads committed repo files (the report drafts and the git-tracked evidence JSONs under output/evidence/, which are NOT bronze and therefore not gitignored) — it does not depend on coursework/ data and needs no tmp_path fixtures because its inputs are first-class committed deliverables; add a module docstring stating this rationale.
6. Update docs/GAP_REGISTER.md GAP-011 row: set Status to in_progress (or closed once the verification command below passes and evidence is recorded), update the Evidence cell to point at output/report/REPORT.md + output/presentation/PRESENTATION.md + tests/test_report_evidence_links.py, and append a row to the 'Test Failure Mapping' table recording the passing pytest command. Update docs/TASKS.md report/draft row status and docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:26 (Report/presentation line) to reflect drafts exist.
7. Run the verification command, confirm green, and record the result in docs/VERIFICATION.md (a new dated subsection mirroring the existing format at lines 24-55).

**Files to touch:** `output/report/REPORT.md (new)`  `output/presentation/PRESENTATION.md (new)`  `tests/test_report_evidence_links.py (new)`  `docs/GAP_REGISTER.md (GAP-011 row + Test Failure Mapping table)`  `docs/TASKS.md (report/draft row status)`  `docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md (line 26 report/presentation status)`  `docs/VERIFICATION.md (new dated results subsection)`

**Definition of Done (contract).**
- [ ] output/report/REPORT.md exists and contains: the proven Gold result (2,968 rows × 4 cols, 151 geos, 1995–2021, AT/HU 27 rows each) with inline evidence citations; the MinIO storage result; the Bronze source coverage table; an explicit 'Known gaps' section linking GAP-013/GAP-006/GAP-009; a Spark placeholder; and an 'Evidence index' claim→path→JSON-key table.
- [ ] output/presentation/PRESENTATION.md exists as a slide outline whose every numeric claim matches REPORT.md figures and cites the same evidence artifacts.
- [ ] Every `output/evidence/...` path referenced in either document resolves to a file that exists on disk (the bronze/ subtrees are gitignored, so the docs must cite manifests/counts/parquet/samples JSON, NOT files under output/evidence/**/bronze/).
- [ ] No number in either document is fabricated or rounded away from its source JSON: each headline figure traces to a key in counts.json / manifest.json / inventory_samples.json / minio-smoke manifest.
- [ ] tests/test_report_evidence_links.py exists, is marked unit, has a docstring justifying that it reads committed deliverables (not coursework/ data), and asserts (a) both docs exist, (b) all cited evidence paths exist, (c) curated headline numbers loaded from the evidence JSON appear verbatim in REPORT.md.
- [ ] `python -m pytest -q tests/test_report_evidence_links.py` passes; `python -m pytest -q` remains green with no new failures (was 87 passed).
- [ ] docs/GAP_REGISTER.md GAP-011 row is updated (status + evidence + a new Test Failure Mapping row), and docs/VERIFICATION.md records the passing command with observed results.

### GAP-012 — Fix the documented Bronze→Gold regen recipe so a clean checkout reproduces the real Gold instead of a silently-empty one

`URGENT [!]` · level **docs** · effort **M** · depends on: none (self-contained; touches docs + pipeline guard + one test). The clean-checkout numeric reproduction needs live network to Eurostat + World Bank endpoints; the automated DoD test must NOT depend on network and uses tmp_path/fixtures.

**Build:** Make the two documented commands (live-check then pipeline) reproduce the headline Gold (2,139×3, AT/HU, WB rail_network_length_km) on a clean checkout, and make a non-existent --bronze-root fail loudly instead of writing an empty Gold.

**Context.** This is the canonical "reproduce the first real Gold" recipe in docs/VERIFICATION.md and the headline evidence for the gold/first-real-result milestone (TASKS.md). A grader or classmate running the two documented commands on a fresh clone is the primary acceptance path for the whole stats spine. Today it silently produces an empty Gold parquet with exit code 0, so the milestone is not actually reproducible. GAP-012 is the highest-severity item in the 2026-06-24 re-audit and is Wave-1 Contract-A blocker before Spark work (TASKS.md:120-128).

**Problem.** Two coupled defects make the documented recipe build an empty Gold without any error.

1) Run-id nesting collides with committed evidence. `output/evidence/local-stats-bronze/manifest.json` IS git-tracked (confirmed: `git ls-files` returns only `manifest.json`), while raw bytes are gitignored by `.gitignore:27` (`output/evidence/**/bronze/`). On a clean checkout `output/evidence/local-stats-bronze/` therefore contains `manifest.json` but no `bronze/`. The first documented command (VERIFICATION.md:35) runs `live_check --out output/evidence/local-stats-bronze`. Inside `run_live_check` (src/railway_lakehouse/bronze/live_check.py:121) it calls `_resolve_run_output_dir(Path(out), run_id)` (live_check.py:645-654): because `(out_path/"manifest.json").exists()` is true, it returns `out_path / run_id` (e.g. `.../local-stats-bronze/live-check-20260624-101500`). The lander then writes the tree to `.../local-stats-bronze/<run_id>/bronze/...` (live_check.py:121-122, 57-65). So the freshly landed bronze is NOT at `.../local-stats-bronze/bronze`.

2) The pipeline command hardcodes the non-nested path and fails silently on a missing root. The second documented command (VERIFICATION.md:36 and the TASKS.md:112 / GAP_REGISTER.md:111-112 evidence row) is `pipeline --bronze-root output/evidence/local-stats-bronze/bronze ...`. That directory does not exist after defect 1. `_read_bronze_stats_frames` (pipeline.py:200-202) routes the `bronze_root` branch to `stats_load.frames_from_bronze(local_root)`. There (silver/stats/load.py:90-95) `base = root/"stats"/source`; `if not base.is_dir(): continue` — a missing root yields `[]` with no error. Empty frames → empty crosswalk → `merge_sources([], …)` → empty `stats_long`. `build_from_silver` (gold/run.py:26-29) calls `build_gold`, whose `pivot_stats` returns `pd.DataFrame(columns=["geo","year"])` on empty input (gold/build.py:55-56), then only logs `WARNING "Gold table is empty"` and still writes the parquet, returning exit 0. `write_gold_counts` (pipeline.py:146-175) then records rows=0. Net effect: the recipe "passes" (exit 0) but the headline Gold is empty.

Note for the fix: an existing unit test pins the current nesting behavior — `tests/test_bronze_live_check.py:166-196` (`test_run_live_check_uses_run_subdirectory_when_output_already_has_evidence`) asserts `manifest_path == out/<run_id>/manifest.json`. The fix must reconcile docs with whatever behavior is chosen (do not silently break that test).

**Steps.**
1. Reproduce the empty Gold first (red state). Simulate a clean checkout for this one evidence dir: in a scratch copy keep only output/evidence/local-stats-bronze/manifest.json (no bronze/). Run the two VERIFICATION.md commands (network up). Observe live_check writes bronze under .../local-stats-bronze/<run_id>/bronze, and the pipeline writes a 0-row parquet with counts rows=0. Capture this as the motivating evidence.
2. Decide the recipe shape. Recommended (least churn, keeps the committed manifest as the audit snapshot and preserves the run-id nesting test): change the DOCUMENTED commands so the live-check writes to a fresh, non-committed output dir and the pipeline reads that same dir's bronze. Concretely document a regen dir like `output/evidence/local-stats-bronze-regen` (gitignored via the existing `output/evidence/**/bronze/` rule for its bronze subtree) for live-check `--out`, and point `--bronze-root` at `<that dir>/bronze`. This avoids the manifest.json collision entirely so `_resolve_run_output_dir` returns the path unchanged.
3. Make the pipeline fail loudly on a non-existent or empty --bronze-root (the durable fix, independent of which dir the docs use). In src/railway_lakehouse/pipeline.py, in `run_pipeline` where `bronze_root` is consumed (pipeline.py:93-95) or at the top of `_read_bronze_stats_frames` (pipeline.py:200), validate the local root: if `bronze_root` is provided and `Path(bronze_root)` does not exist, raise a `ValueError`/`FileNotFoundError` with the offending path and a hint to run the live-check first. Additionally, after reading stats frames (pipeline.py:106-107), if the local-Bronze branch returned zero stats frames AND zero news articles for a stats-intended run, raise rather than proceed to write an empty Gold. Keep the message actionable (mention --bronze-root and the live-check command). Do NOT change raw Bronze landing semantics or the lander.
4. Tighten the empty-Gold guard at the writer boundary. In gold/run.py `build_from_silver` (gold/run.py:26-29) the empty case is only a WARNING. Leave Gold importable/pure, but ensure the PIPELINE path does not silently emit a 0-row headline parquet: enforce the non-empty check in the pipeline (step 3) so library callers that legitimately want empty Gold are unaffected. (If the team prefers, add an explicit `allow_empty: bool = False` flag to build_from_silver and have the pipeline pass allow_empty=False; the pipeline raising in step 3 is sufficient and lower-risk.)
5. Rewrite the documented recipe in docs/VERIFICATION.md (lines 31-54). Replace the two commands so that: (a) live-check `--out` targets the fresh regen dir, (b) `--bronze-root` matches `<regen-dir>/bronze`, (c) keep `--max-artifacts 1 --timeout-seconds 60`, `--skip-news-extraction --news 0`, `--counts-out ...`. Re-state the observed counts as the contract: 2,139 rows × 3 cols, columns [geo, year, rail_network_length_km], AT and HU present, year range 1995-2021 (matching GAP_REGISTER.md:40 closure text and the current VERIFICATION.md:47-53 observed block). Add one sentence explaining the committed manifest.json is the audit snapshot and raw bronze must be regenerated because it is gitignored (.gitignore:27).
6. Sync the other two doc references to the new path so they cannot drift back: GAP_REGISTER.md test-failure row (line 111-112) and any TASKS.md mention (TASKS.md:104-106) of the recipe. Do not alter committed numeric evidence; only fix the command path.
7. Add the deterministic DoD test (see verification). Put it in tests/test_pipeline_gaps.py (integration marker already set at module level, line 9) using tmp_path fixtures only — no coursework/ or output/ data. It must (a) assert that pipeline.main/run_pipeline with a non-existent --bronze-root raises (not writes empty Gold), and (b) assert that a tmp Bronze tree built under <tmp>/<run_id>/bronze by live_check is NOT found at <tmp>/bronze (locking the nesting contract the docs now respect). Optionally reuse tests/fixtures/bronze to prove the corrected path shape yields a non-empty Gold.
8. Run the full verification command set and record results in VERIFICATION.md and the GAP_REGISTER test-failure table; flip GAP-012 to closed only after the clean-checkout regen actually writes the non-empty parquet + counts.json and the new test passes.

**Files to touch:** `src/railway_lakehouse/pipeline.py`  `src/railway_lakehouse/gold/run.py`  `docs/VERIFICATION.md`  `docs/GAP_REGISTER.md`  `docs/TASKS.md`  `tests/test_pipeline_gaps.py`

**Definition of Done (contract).**
- [ ] On a clean checkout (only output/evidence/local-stats-bronze/manifest.json present, no bronze/), running the two documented commands in order with network up writes a NON-empty headline parquet and counts.json: rows=2139, columns=3, column_names include rail_network_length_km, contains_AT=true, contains_HU=true, year_min=1995, year_max=2021 (matches GAP_REGISTER.md:40).
- [ ] A non-existent --bronze-root no longer produces a 0-row Gold with exit 0: pipeline raises a clear error (path + hint to run live-check) OR refuses to write empty Gold. Verified by an automated test, not just manually.
- [ ] docs/VERIFICATION.md commands and GAP_REGISTER.md:111-112 / TASKS.md recipe references all point at the same working --out / --bronze-root pair; no path drift remains.
- [ ] New deterministic test in tests/test_pipeline_gaps.py passes: it asserts (a) missing --bronze-root raises, (b) live_check nests under <out>/<run_id> when <out> already holds a manifest.json (the docs honor this). Test uses tmp_path/fixtures only.
- [ ] Existing test tests/test_bronze_live_check.py:166 (run-id nesting) still passes — the fix did not silently change live_check nesting semantics.
- [ ] python -m pytest -q is green (no new xfails); python -m compileall -q src tests passes; git diff --check clean.
- [ ] Hard rules respected: raw Bronze landing semantics unchanged; numeric stat merge stays deterministic (no LLM rewriting numbers); no fabricated rows; all new artifacts under output/ ; tests independent of coursework/ data.

**Verify:** `Primary automated gate: `python -m pytest -q -m integration` (must be green and include the new GAP-012 test). Full guard: `python -m pytest -q && python -m compileall -q src tests && git diff --check`. Clean-checkout repro (network up), using the regen dir the new docs specify, e.g.: `python -m railway_lakehouse.bronze.live_check --sources eurostat,worldbank --out output/evidence/local-stats-bronze-regen --max-artifacts 1 --timeout-seconds 60` then `python -m railway_lakehouse.pipeline --bronze-root output/evidence/local-stats-bronze-regen/bronze --skip-news-extraction --news 0 --out output/evidence/local-stats-bronze-regen/railway_ml.parquet --crosswalk-path output/evidence/local-stats-bronze-regen/crosswalk_cache.json --counts-out output/evidence/local-stats-bronze-regen/counts.json` then `python -m json.tool output/evidence/local-stats-bronze-regen/counts.json` and assert rows=2139, columns=3, rail_network_length_km present, AT/HU true, 1995-2021. Negative check: `python -m railway_lakehouse.pipeline --bronze-root output/evidence/does-not-exist/bronze --skip-news-extraction --news 0 --out /tmp/empty.parquet` must exit non-zero with a clear path error, not write a 0-row parquet.`

**Pitfalls.** ["Do not 'fix' this by committing the raw bronze bytes — they are intentionally gitignored (.gitignore:27) and large (~15 MB); the contract is regenerate-from-manifest. Keep raw Bronze immutable and out of git.", "Do not change `_resolve_run_output_dir` nesting to make the old hardcoded path work — that would break tests/test_bronze_live_check.py:166-196 which pins the nesting-on-existing-evidence behavior, and would risk clobbering the committed manifest snapshot. Fix the DOCS to use a fresh dir instead.", "Keep gold/build.py and the merge deterministic: the empty-Gold guard must live on the pipeline/CLI boundary, not inside the pure builder — other callers (silver persist→Gold integration test) may legitimately produce small/empty frames. Prefer raising in pipeline.run_pipeline over hard-failing build_gold.", "Do not let an LLM touch numbers anywhere in this path; the crosswalk LLM step is gated by ollama_reachable and is irrelevant here (recipe uses --skip-news-extraction --news 0).", "Windows path handling: bronze paths are globbed with both / and \\ normalized (pipeline.py:248-266, load.py:90); keep new error messages using as_posix() to match existing style.", "The counts.json contract (pipeline.py:146-175) keys on column presence; if Eurostat ever starts mapping (GAP-013/GAP-023) the column count could change — assert the WB feature and AT/HU presence as the stable invariant, plus the documented 2,139×3 as the current snapshot, not a brittle exact-column-list-only check.", "Network flakiness: the 2026-06-24 re-audit saw a transient Eurostat RemoteDisconnected (GAP_REGISTER.md:119); the clean-checkout repro is network-dependent, so gate CLOSURE on the World Bank feature + counts, and keep the deterministic test (which proves the guard + nesting) as the real regression lock."]

### GAP-017 — Pin a coherent Spark stack (Spark 4.1 + delta-spark 4.x + S3A Maven hadoop-aws 3.4.1 + JDK 17/21) and add a deterministic version-guard test

`URGENT [!]` · level **spark** · effort **M** · depends on: none (Wave-1 prerequisite). GAP-018 (pyproject pandas/pyarrow bounds + lockfile) is a sibling in the SAME Wave-1 batch and touches the same pyproject.toml — coordinate so the spark extra edit (this gap) and the core-deps bounds edit (GAP-018) do not collide; they touch different blocks (lines 26-28 vs 11-13). GAP-009 spark/evidence-job depends on THIS gap being done first.

**Build:** Replace the unbounded `pyspark>=3.5` extra with a pinned, internally-consistent Spark 4.1 stack that is compatible with the repo's actual Python 3.14 / pandas 3.0 / pyarrow 24 environment, record the JDK choice in README + docs + .env.example, and add a deterministic `tests/test_spark_stack_pins.py` guard so the stack can never silently drift again.

**Context.** Spark is the headline "Big Data technology" deliverable (GAP-009 `spark/evidence-job`) and the report's centerpiece (GAP-011). GAP-017 is the Wave-1 prerequisite that unblocks it: before any Spark job is written, the dependency stack must resolve to ONE coherent, installable set of versions whose JDK, Hadoop, and Delta generations all agree. Right now they do not — and worse, the documented "fix" (Spark 3.5.x) is itself incompatible with the repo's own runtime, so this gap needs a real version-selection decision, not just a `==` pin of the documented numbers.

**Problem.** `pyproject.toml:26-28` declares the Spark extra as:

```toml
spark = [
  "pyspark>=3.5",
]
```

`>=3.5` is unbounded. On this machine `python -m pip index versions pyspark` resolves it to **4.1.2** (verified), which is the trap GAP-017 (`docs/GAP_REGISTER.md:45`) describes: a plain `pip install .[spark]` silently pulls Spark 4.1.x, which (a) won't start on the installed Java 8 (`java -version` => `1.8.0_491`, `JAVA_HOME` unset) and (b) is incompatible with the stale Spark-3/Delta-3/Hadoop-3.3 generation previously written in the docs.

The documented Stack-A remedy is NOT viable in this repo, and this is the load-bearing finding: the repo's actual runtime, verified live, is **Python 3.14.0 / pandas 3.0.3 / pyarrow 24.0.0 / numpy 2.4.4** (matches `docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:288` "Env: Python 3.14.0 / pandas 3.0.3 / pyarrow 24.0.0"), and all 87 tests pass on it. The older PySpark line cannot run on Python 3.14 (Spark 4.1 is the first release to support Python 3.14) and its PyPI floors (pandas<… / pyarrow>=… of an older generation) collide with pandas 3.0 / pyarrow 24. So pinning Stack A would force a Python + pandas + pyarrow downgrade that breaks the already-green pipeline — violating "preserve user changes" and re-opening GAP-018's stack-coherence concern.

There is also no version-guard test (`tests/test_env_versions.py` referenced by sibling GAP-018 does not exist) and no committed lock/constraints file, so nothing prevents the next clean install from drifting again. The GAP-017 closure criterion explicitly permits the alternative path: "**or** deliberately bump the whole stack to Spark 4 + delta-spark 4.x; record the chosen JDK (17) at manifest/README level."

DECISION (chosen, not left open): adopt the coherent **Spark 4.1 stack (Stack B-current)**, because it is the only stack installable on the repo's existing Python 3.14 / pandas 3.0 / pyarrow 24 runtime, and it matches the greenfield research recommendation (Spark 4.1.2; ANSI-on-by-default is a net data-integrity win; window-function + Parquet APIs are unchanged 3.5→4.x so migration risk is ~zero). Concretely pin pip packages only: `pyspark==4.1.*` (resolves 4.1.2) and `delta-spark==4.1.*` (Delta 4.1.x / 4.3.0, built on Spark 4.1.0). Record the Spark Maven coordinates for runtime sessions: Delta `io.delta:delta-spark_4.1_2.13:4.1.0`, S3A `org.apache.hadoop:hadoop-aws:3.4.1,software.amazon.awssdk:bundle:2.24.6` (the Hadoop connector must equal Spark 4.x's bundled hadoop-client 3.4.1), and **JDK 17 or 21** (set `JAVA_HOME`). This supersedes the Stack-A numbers currently written in `docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md` and `docs/index.html`, which must be rewritten so docs and code agree (the closure criterion requires the chosen JDK recorded at README level).

**Steps.**
1. 1. Re-confirm the live environment so the spec's premise is current (it can change between sessions): run `python --version`, `python -c "import pandas,pyarrow,numpy;print(pandas.__version__,pyarrow.__version__,numpy.__version__)"`, `java -version`, `echo $JAVA_HOME`. Expect Python 3.14.x / pandas 3.0.x / pyarrow 24.x / Java 8 / JAVA_HOME unset. If Python is actually <=3.12 AND pandas <2.3-era, Stack A becomes viable and you must STOP and re-decide with the user — but on the verified state, proceed with Stack B.

Add a short `# GAP-017:` comment above the block stating the JDK requirement (17 or 21) and that S3A uses Maven coordinates from `railway_lakehouse.spark_config`, not pip dependencies. Do NOT touch the core `dependencies` block (pandas/pyarrow bounds are GAP-018's job — leave them for that gap to avoid a merge collision in the same Wave-1 batch).
3. 3. Add a deterministic guard test `tests/test_spark_stack_pins.py` modeled exactly on `tests/test_infra_minio.py` (same `pytestmark = pytest.mark.unit`, same `ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]`, parse committed files rather than importing pyspark). It must NOT import pyspark (pyspark is an optional, possibly-uninstalled extra). ## HIGH

### GAP-006 — Silver Stats: KSH XLSX → StatFact reader (wire the dormant read_tabular_long helper into frames_from_bronze)

`HIGH` · level **silver** · effort **M** · depends on: none (this is a self-contained additive Silver reader; silver/persist-contract and silver/persist-outputs — GAP-006 prerequisites — are already done per docs/TASKS.md:80,83 and docs/GAP_REGISTER.md:22). It does NOT depend on infra/ollama-model because the deterministic test path uses use_llm=False / rule-based English-label crosswalk.

**Build:** Add a deterministic KSH (Hungarian STADAT) XLSX → StatFact Silver reader that turns already-landed Bronze KSH workbook bytes into HU StatFact long rows, register it in the stats loader dispatch, and prove it with a tmp_path-built fixture XLSX test — advancing GAP-006 from 2/5 toward 3/5 stats parsers.

**Context.** GAP-006 (Silver) closure requires "KSH/Statistik Austria/UIC fixture parser tests pass" (docs/GAP_REGISTER.md:22). Today only 2 of 5 stats parsers exist (Eurostat + World Bank); KSH/StatAustria/UIC are listed as "MISSING — no reader" in docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:70-72. KSH bytes already land verbatim in Bronze (src/railway_lakehouse/bronze/sources/ksh.py lands 6 confirmed rail STADAT XLSX tables under stats/ksh/<dataset_id>/ingest_date=.../<code>.xlsx), and a dormant generic reader read_tabular_long already exists (src/railway_lakehouse/silver/stats/merge.py:92-106) but is never called. This task wires the first national-source reader (KSH, the best-documented: 6 tables, per-table feature_hint, HU-only geo, English STADAT headers) into the Silver stats load dispatch (src/railway_lakehouse/silver/stats/load.py:76-79, 87-111) that the pipeline already calls via _read_bronze_stats_frames (src/railway_lakehouse/pipeline.py:200-202). It sits squarely on the Bronze→Silver→Gold spine: KSH StatFact rows flow through merge_sources → build_from_silver → the (geo,year) Gold matrix, giving a second real HU stats source alongside World Bank.

**Problem.** The stats loader src/railway_lakehouse/silver/stats/load.py:76-79 registers only worldbank and eurostat in its `_SOURCES` dispatch table; `frames_from_bronze` (load.py:87-111) therefore walks `stats/worldbank` and `stats/eurostat` only. A Bronze tree containing `stats/ksh/ksh_rail_network/ingest_date=.../sza0030.xlsx` is silently skipped — zero KSH rows ever reach Silver or Gold, despite the bytes being landed live (evidence: output/evidence/ksh-live-check-2026-06-22-current/manifest.json, 6 XLSX, 92,509 B). The intended integration point, `read_tabular_long(df, dataset_id, *, geo, label_col, year_col, value_col, unit)` at merge.py:92-106, expects an ALREADY-tidy (label, year, value) frame; the missing piece is the XLSX-specific step that (a) reads workbook bytes into a DataFrame (needs an Excel engine — `openpyxl` is NOT currently installed; verified `ModuleNotFoundError: No module named 'openpyxl'`, and it is absent from pyproject.toml:11-20), and (b) reshapes a STADAT wide-by-year sheet into the tidy frame read_tabular_long consumes. StatFact.source_system already enumerates `ksh` (schema.py:14) and Gold SOURCE_PRIORITY already ranks `ksh` (gold/build.py:30), so downstream is ready; only the Silver reader and its registration are missing.

**Steps.**
1. Add the Excel engine dependency: in pyproject.toml [project].dependencies (pyproject.toml:11-20) add `openpyxl>=3.1` (pandas needs an engine to read .xlsx; it is a light pure-Python dep, no native build). Then run `python -m pip install -e ".[test]"` so the editable env picks it up. Do NOT add odfpy/pdfplumber here — StatAustria ODS and UIC PDF are explicitly deferred (docs/TASKS.md:95, Stage 4 / Wave 5) and out of scope for this single-session task.
2. In src/railway_lakehouse/silver/stats/merge.py, keep read_tabular_long (merge.py:92-106) as the tidy-frame entry point. It already coerces year/value numerically with errors='coerce' and tags source_dataset/source_column — do NOT change its numeric handling (Hard Rule: deterministic numeric parsing, no LLM touching numbers).
3. Add a new deterministic reader `load_ksh_frame(raw: bytes, dataset_id: str) -> pd.DataFrame` to src/railway_lakehouse/silver/stats/load.py, mirroring load_eurostat_frame/load_worldbank_frame (load.py:39-71). Steps inside: (1) read the workbook from bytes via `pd.read_excel(io.BytesIO(raw), sheet_name=0, header=None, engine='openpyxl', dtype=object)` so no value is silently cast; (2) deterministically locate the header year row and the label column for a STADAT 'wide years across columns, feature label in a leading column' layout — detect the year columns as the cells in the header region that parse as 4-digit years (1900..2100) via pd.to_numeric, and treat the first non-year text column as label_col; (3) melt to a tidy long (label, year, value) frame; (4) call merge.read_tabular_long(tidy, dataset_id, geo='HU', label_col='label', year_col='year', value_col='value', unit='ksh_native'); (5) tag `frame['source_system']='ksh'`; (6) on an unparseable/empty/non-XLSX body return `_empty()` (load.py:35-37) and logger.warning — never fabricate rows (Hard Rule: do not fabricate data). Guard the XLSX magic (`raw[:4] == b'PK\x03\x04'`) before read_excel and treat a non-match as empty, reusing the same posture as bronze/sources/ksh.py:114-130 looks_like_xlsx.
4. Register KSH in the `_SOURCES` dispatch in load.py:76-79: add `"ksh": (load_ksh_frame, (".xlsx",)),`. This makes frames_from_bronze (load.py:87-111) automatically walk `stats/ksh/<dataset_id>/ingest_date=*/...` and pick the latest partition, with no other change needed (the `_`-prefixed skip and meta.json skip at load.py:97,103-104 already apply).
5. Confirm the crosswalk maps KSH English STADAT labels deterministically WITHOUT the LLM: the rule table _ENGLISH_LABEL_RULES (merge.py:155-176) already covers 'network'→rail_network_length_km, 'freight'/'goods'→rail_freight_tonnes, 'passenger'→rail_passengers, 'rolling stock'→rail_rolling_stock, etc. Because KSH is fetched from the English STADAT endpoint (/sza/en/, bronze/sources/ksh.py:8,29), the fixture labels MUST be English STADAT headers so build_crosswalk(use_llm=False) maps them by rule (merge.py:178-205). Do not add a hardcoded KSH-specific crosswalk; rely on the existing English rule path. If a label has no rule it stays 'unmapped' and is dropped+logged (merge.py:218-221) — that is the correct visible-unmapped behavior the contract demands.
6. Add a deterministic unit/integration test file tests/test_silver_stats_ksh.py marked `pytestmark = pytest.mark.unit` (it touches no network/services). In a fixture, BUILD a tiny KSH-shaped .xlsx in tmp_path using openpyxl (a header row with a label column header plus year columns 2019/2020/2021, then 1-2 data rows with English labels like 'Length of railway lines' and 'Goods transported by rail'), serialize to bytes via a BytesIO/save, and assert: (a) load_ksh_frame(bytes,'ksh_rail_network') returns a non-empty long frame with columns [geo,year,value,unit,source_dataset,source_column,source_system], geo=='HU', source_system=='ksh', unit=='ksh_native', and the numeric values pass through verbatim (e.g. exact float equality on a known cell); (b) build a Bronze tree under tmp_path (stats/ksh/ksh_rail_network/ingest_date=2026-06-22/sza0030.xlsx) and assert stats_load.frames_from_bronze(tmp_path) now returns a ksh frame; (c) end-to-end via stats_load.build_silver_stats(tmp_path, use_llm=False, out=...) (load.py:114-134) with CROSSWALK_PATH monkeypatched to a tmp file (pattern from tests/test_silver_stats_integration.py:24-31): assert a known English KSH label maps to its canonical feature and value is preserved, AND a deliberately non-rail label (e.g. 'Road network') ends up 'unmapped' in the crosswalk cache and absent from the unified output (mirrors the CO2 unmapped assertion at tests/test_silver_stats_integration.py:60-65). Use tmp_path/openpyxl only — never read coursework/ or output/evidence/ data (Hard Rule).
7. Update docs to reflect the new reader: in docs/STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md flip the KSH row in the Data Inventory table (line 70) from 'MISSING — no XLSX reader' to a parsed state, bump 'Stats parsers to StatFact: 2/5' (line 33) to 3/5, and update Original Task #9 status (line 105) from '2/5' to '3/5'. In docs/GAP_REGISTER.md update the GAP-006 Evidence cell (line 22) to record that KSH XLSX→StatFact now has a fixture-backed reader+test. Add the verification command + result to the Test Failure Mapping table (docs/GAP_REGISTER.md:64+).
8. Run the verification commands (see verification field) and confirm green before claiming done.

### GAP-007 — Wire gold/run.py to load persisted Silver Parquet and emit Gold + row/column counts

`HIGH` · level **gold** · effort **S** · depends on: silver/persist-outputs (DONE) — provides persist.load_stats/load_news and the frozen Silver Parquet path contract (silver/persist.py; docs/DATA_CONTRACTS.md:70-98). No code blockers remain; GAP-007 is purely the CLI wiring + counts + test.

**Build:** Replace the placeholder `gold.run main()` with a CLI that reads persisted Silver (`load_stats`/`load_news`) from a `--silver-root`, calls `build_from_silver`, writes the Gold Parquet under `output/`, and records a row/column `counts.json`; add a deterministic integration test proving fixture Silver inputs produce Gold Parquet + counts.

**Context.** Gold is the analysis-ready feature matrix that the graded Spark job (GAP-009) reads. Today Gold's deterministic transform logic (`gold/build.py`) is complete and tested, and the Silver persistence read/write layer (`silver/persist.py`) is done and tested, but the two are only ever joined in-memory inside `pipeline.run_pipeline` — `gold.run`'s own CLI is a stub that never touches storage. GAP-007 closes the lakehouse handoff: Gold must be runnable directly off the persisted Silver Parquet tree (`silver/.../*.parquet`) with no in-memory dependency, which is also the clean input boundary the Spark evidence job needs. This sits between `silver/persist-outputs` (done) and `spark/evidence-job` in the pipeline (docs/TASKS.md:83-86).

**Problem.** `src/railway_lakehouse/gold/run.py` main() (lines 32-39) is a placeholder: it builds an ArgumentParser with only `--out`, `--year-min`, `--year-max`, calls `ap.parse_args()` (discarding the result), then just logs "gold.run: load Silver stats_long + news_rows from your storage, then call build_from_silver(...). Wire MinIO/Parquet reads here." It never reads Silver and never produces Gold. The module docstring (run.py:6-11) explicitly defers the Silver read as a "wiring point". The read primitives already exist and are tested: `persist.load_stats(root)` / `persist.load_news(root)` return the canonical StatFact/NewsFeature frames from the latest `ingest_date=` partition (silver/persist.py:170-185), and `build_from_silver(stats_long, news_rows, out_path, year_min, year_max)` is the pure, importable, already-tested entry point (gold/run.py:23-29). The persist->reload->Gold contract is even green as a library call in tests/test_silver_persist_integration.py, but there is no CLI wiring and no counts artifact from `gold.run` (closure requires "recorded row/column counts"). STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:308-311 confirms: "the pipeline still never calls persist.py before Gold (GAP-007). The persist->reload->Gold contract is green only in an isolated test, not in the production pipeline." docs/GAP_REGISTER.md:23 is the authoritative row.

**Steps.**
1. Read the four anchors to lock the contract: gold/run.py:23-43 (build_from_silver + stub main), silver/persist.py:170-185 (load_stats/load_news semantics: latest partition unless ingest_date given; empty -> 0-row schema-shaped frame), pipeline.py:146-175 (write_gold_counts shape to mirror), tests/test_silver_persist_integration.py (the persist->reload->Gold pattern to lift into a CLI-level test).
2. Decide the counts writer: reuse the existing pipeline.write_gold_counts (pipeline.py:146-175) rather than duplicate it. Move it to a shared, import-cycle-safe location OR import it into gold/run.py. Cleanest: import `from railway_lakehouse.pipeline import write_gold_counts` is acceptable since pipeline already imports gold (gold has no back-import to pipeline today, so importing pipeline from gold/run would create the cycle). To avoid the cycle, extract `write_gold_counts` into `gold/build.py` as `write_gold_counts(parquet_path, counts_out)` (pure pandas, no new deps) and have pipeline.py import it from there; update pipeline.py's local def to delegate or be replaced by the import. This keeps Gold self-contained and lets gold.run call it without importing pipeline.
3. Rewrite `gold/run.py` main(): add args `--silver-root` (required; local Silver tree root that contains stats/stat_fact/... and news/news_feature/...), `--out` (default to an output/-rooted path, e.g. `output/evidence/gold/railway_ml.parquet`, never `gold/...`), `--ingest-date` (optional; forwarded to load_stats/load_news; default None => latest partition), `--year-min`, `--year-max` (int, optional), `--counts-out` (optional; JSON row/col summary path). Parse argv (accept argv param for testability, mirroring pipeline.main(argv=None)).
4. In main(): call `stats_long = persist.load_stats(silver_root, ingest_date=ingest_date)` and `news_df = persist.load_news(silver_root, ingest_date=ingest_date)`. Convert news to the row form build_gold expects: `news_rows = news_df.to_dict('records')` (build.aggregate_news/_news_to_df accept dicts; gold/build.py:71 handles dict-or-object). Call `out_path = build_from_silver(stats_long, news_rows, out, year_min=year_min, year_max=year_max)`.
5. If `--counts-out` given, call the counts writer on out_path and log the counts path (reuse the GAP-010 evidence pattern). build_from_silver already logs a warning when Gold is empty (gold/run.py:27-28) — keep that; do NOT silently write an empty Gold without the warning (mirrors the GAP-012 lesson about silent-empty Gold).
6. Ensure `main(argv=None)` returns the out_path string (so the test can assert on the return value, matching pipeline.main()'s contract).
7. Update the module docstring (gold/run.py:1-11) to document the real command, e.g. `python -m railway_lakehouse.gold.run --silver-root output/evidence/silver --out output/evidence/gold/railway_ml.parquet --counts-out output/evidence/gold/counts.json`, and remove the 'Wire MinIO/Parquet reads here' deferral language.
8. Add a deterministic integration test `tests/test_gold_load_from_silver.py` marked `pytest.mark.integration`. In it: build a unified StatFact frame from the committed Bronze fixtures via `stats_load.build_silver_stats(FIXTURES, use_llm=False)` (monkeypatch stats_merge.CROSSWALK_PATH to tmp_path to keep the cache isolated, as test_silver_persist_integration.py does) OR construct a small StatFact DataFrame inline; persist it with `persist.persist_silver(stats_long, news_rows, silver_root, ingest_date='2026-06-23')` into a tmp_path silver tree; then invoke `gold.run.main(['--silver-root', str(silver_root), '--out', str(tmp_path/'gold'/'railway_ml.parquet'), '--counts-out', str(tmp_path/'gold'/'counts.json'), '--ingest-date', '2026-06-23'])`. Use only tmp_path + tests/fixtures/bronze — never coursework/ data.

- [ ] `python -m pytest -q -m integration` passes (new test included); `python -m pytest -q` passes with no regressions (current baseline: 87 passed per GAP_REGISTER.md:116).
- [ ] Empty Silver inputs still log the 'Gold table is empty' warning (gold/run.py:27-28) rather than silently writing an empty Gold with no signal.

### GAP-010 — Make the live (MinIO/s3) stats branch read World Bank + Eurostat so a genuinely-live Bronze→Silver→Gold run produces a feature-bearing Gold

`HIGH` · level **pipeline** · effort **M** · depends on: none (the change is self-contained; fsspec 2024.6.1 with a working memory:// filesystem is already installed and confirmed), Co-dependent (do NOT bundle, but reference): GAP-012 — the documented --bronze-root regen recipe nests output under a run_id when a committed manifest.json/bronze exists (bronze/live_check._resolve_run_output_dir, live_check.py:645-654); the optional live verification step must target a clean out dir to avoid the empty-Gold trap., Informational: GAP-020 (s3/MinIO read-back has no deterministic coverage) is partially advanced by this task's memory:// test but is broader (covers _read_text/_read_tsv s3 branches and gzip-over-s3); does not need to be fully closed here.

**Build:** Replace the Eurostat-only live-MinIO fallback in pipeline._read_bronze_stats_frames with an s3-capable stats reader that loads both World Bank JSON and Eurostat TSV from the Bronze bucket, so a no---bronze-root MinIO run yields the same World Bank Gold features the local-root path already produces.

**Context.** GAP-010 ("S4 live Bronze/Silver/Gold run", status in_progress) is the umbrella gap proving an end-to-end run over real object storage. As of 2026-06-24 the MinIO object store is live-proven (docker compose up + scripts/minio_smoke.py round-trip passed) and a World Bank Bronze→Silver→Gold run produced a real 2,968×4 Gold — but ONLY via the local --bronze-root path. The GAP-010 row itself names the blocker to a genuinely-live Gold: "the live MinIO stats branch drops World Bank" (tracked as the child GAP-013, pipeline.py:200-210). This sits on the data spine Bronze→Silver→Gold, immediately before the Spark deliverable (GAP-009); a feature-less live Gold would make the live-E2E claim in the report indefensible.

**Problem.** In src/railway_lakehouse/pipeline.py, _read_bronze_stats_frames (lines 193-210) branches on whether the lander exposes bronze_root. Local mode (line 201-202) calls stats_load.frames_from_bronze(local_root) which reads BOTH worldbank and eurostat (see silver/stats/load.py:76-79 _SOURCES, frames_from_bronze:87-111). The live/MinIO branch (lines 204-209) instead calls _read_bronze_eurostat(lander) (pipeline.py:178-189), which only globs domain="stats", source="eurostat" via _list_bronze_files (pipeline.py:248-261) and melts via stats_merge.read_eurostat_tsv. World Bank — the ONLY source that currently maps to a Gold feature (rail_network_length_km, rail_freight_tonne_km; Eurostat is dropped for an unrelated SDMX-header reason noted in STATE_AND_ROADMAP.md:299-308) — is never read in live mode. Result: a real MinIO run (lander = RawLander() with .s3, no bronze_root) silently produces a stats-feature-less Gold, while the only feature-bearing Gold to date came from --bronze-root. Root cause: frames_from_bronze in silver/stats/load.py is Path-only (line 90 root = Path(root); line 94 base.is_dir(); line 96 base.iterdir(); line 107 f.read_bytes()) so it cannot walk an fsspec/s3fs filesystem, forcing the Eurostat-only shortcut. The live read-back path (lander.s3.glob / lander.s3.open) also has zero deterministic test coverage (overlaps GAP-020).

**Steps.**
1. Read the three anchor functions to confirm contracts before editing: pipeline.py _read_bronze_stats_frames (193-210), _read_bronze_eurostat (178-189), _list_bronze_files/_read_tsv/_read_text (248-281); silver/stats/load.py frames_from_bronze (87-111) and the byte-level loaders load_worldbank_frame (39-57) + load_eurostat_frame (60-71) which already take raw bytes; silver/stats/merge.py read_worldbank_json (77-89) and read_eurostat_tsv (59-74).
2. Add an s3-capable frame reader in silver/stats/load.py that mirrors frames_from_bronze but walks an fsspec filesystem. Signature: frames_from_bronze_s3(fs, bucket: str) -> list[pd.DataFrame]. For each (source, (loader, suffixes)) in the existing _SOURCES dict, build base prefix f"{bucket}/stats/{source}"; if not fs.exists(base) continue; enumerate dataset dirs, skip names starting with '_' (catalogue), pick the latest ingest_date= partition by lexical sort (same rule as _latest_partition:82-84, which works because ISO dates sort correctly), then for each non-.meta.json file whose name ends with an accepted suffix call loader(fs.cat_file(path) or fs.open(path,'rb').read(), dataset_id) and append non-empty frames. Reuse the exact same _SOURCES, suffix-filtering, '_'-prefix skip and .meta.json skip as the Path version so local and live stay behaviorally identical — DO NOT duplicate the loaders. Log loaded frame count like the Path version (load.py:110).
3. Refactor to avoid divergence: extract the shared walk into a small private helper that takes generic (list_dataset_dirs, list_partition_files, read_bytes) callables, OR keep two thin wrappers (frames_from_bronze for Path, frames_from_bronze_s3 for fsspec) that both feed the same loaders. Prefer the helper so the '_'-prefix skip, suffix filter, latest-partition rule, and empty-frame guard exist once. Keep frames_from_bronze's public signature unchanged (callers: pipeline.py:202, silver/stats/load.py:120 build_silver_stats).
4. Rewrite the live branch of pipeline._read_bronze_stats_frames (currently 204-209). Replace the _read_bronze_eurostat-only fallback with: require the lander expose .s3 (mirror the existing guard at _list_bronze_files:256-257 raising ValueError('lander must expose either bronze_root or s3')); call stats_load.frames_from_bronze_s3(lander.s3, BRONZE_BUCKET) (BRONZE_BUCKET is already imported at pipeline.py:24). After collecting frames, count distinct source_system values and log.warning if zero worldbank frames were returned (this is the GAP-013 'live branch WARNs on zero WB frames' closure clause). Keep the bronze_root branch (201-202) exactly as-is.
5. Decide _read_bronze_eurostat's fate. It is now unused by the stats path but is still directly asserted by tests/test_pipeline_gaps.py:18,21-26 against the local fixture. Keep the function (it still works for the local Path fixture and is part of the tested surface), but ensure the live stats path no longer calls it. Do not delete it in this task — that would break test_pipeline_bronze_readers_load_local_fixtures.
6. Update the now-stale docstring/comments that assert the Eurostat-only fallback: pipeline.py:104-105 ('Live MinIO mode keeps the existing Eurostat-only fallback for now.') and pipeline.py:197-198 (same in _read_bronze_stats_frames docstring). State that live mode now reads all _SOURCES (World Bank + Eurostat) from the bucket via fsspec, identical to local mode.
7. Add a deterministic, Docker-free test (the DoD test) in tests/test_pipeline_gaps.py (it already carries pytestmark = pytest.mark.integration at line 9 and imports SimpleNamespace). Build an in-memory fsspec filesystem: import fsspec; fs = fsspec.filesystem('memory'); seed it under f'{BRONZE_BUCKET}/stats/worldbank/IS.RRS.PASG.KM/ingest_date=2026-06-22/IS.RRS.PASG.KM.json' and f'{BRONZE_BUCKET}/stats/eurostat/rail_passengers_demo/ingest_date=2026-06-22/passengers.tsv' by copying the bytes of the committed fixtures under tests/fixtures/bronze/stats/ (read with Path.read_bytes, write with fs.pipe_file / fs.open('wb')). Drive pipeline._read_bronze_stats_frames(SimpleNamespace(s3=fs)) and assert a worldbank source_system frame is present (the core GAP-013 assertion). Add a second assertion that local (SimpleNamespace(bronze_root=FIXTURE_BRONZE)) and live (memory fs) return the same set of source_system values — the local/live parity check.
8. Add a negative-path test asserting the no-backend guard still fires: pipeline._read_bronze_stats_frames(SimpleNamespace()) raises ValueError mentioning bronze_root or s3 (mirrors the existing _list_bronze_files guard).
9. Run the full suite and the integration marker subset; confirm green (current baseline is 87 passed, see GAP_REGISTER.md:116). Update the GAP_REGISTER.md GAP-013 row to closed with the evidence line, and add a Test Failure Mapping row, and bump GAP-010's row note to reflect that the live stats branch now reads World Bank. Mention the remaining GAP-010 follow-ups (Ollama/news live extraction, Spark, and the GAP-012 regen-recipe fix) stay open.
10. Optional but recommended for a true live demo (only if MinIO is up, do NOT block the DoD on it): docker compose up -d; python -m railway_lakehouse.bronze.live_check --sources worldbank --out output/evidence/<dated-dir> --max-artifacts 2 (mind GAP-012: point at a CLEAN out dir with no committed manifest.json/bronze so _resolve_run_output_dir at bronze/live_check.py:645-654 does not nest under a run_id), then run python -m railway_lakehouse.pipeline (no --bronze-root) --skip-news-extraction --news 0 --out output/evidence/<dir>/railway_ml.parquet --counts-out .../counts.json and confirm rail_network_length_km / rail_freight_tonne_km appear. Record the command + counts in GAP_REGISTER.md Test Failure Mapping.

### GAP-013 — Live MinIO stats path must land and read World Bank, not just Eurostat

`HIGH` · level **pipeline** · effort **M** · depends on: none (independent of the other re-audit gaps). Coordinate with GAP-014 (forces UTF-8 on the s3 _read_text path) and GAP-020 (s3 read-back test coverage) since all three touch pipeline.py:248-281 — keep the new World Bank reader on a bytes path (`_read_bytes`) so it does not collide with GAP-014's text-encoding change. Loosely related to GAP-012 (the regen recipe), but GAP-013 is fixable and testable without it.

**Build:** Add a deterministic World Bank reader to the live/s3 branch of `_read_bronze_stats_frames` so a genuinely-live MinIO Bronze->Silver->Gold run produces a non-empty stats matrix (today it silently drops World Bank, the only source mapping to a Gold feature).

**Context.** This sits at the Bronze->Silver hand-off in the live (MinIO/s3) execution path of the end-to-end pipeline (`src/railway_lakehouse/pipeline.py`). The deterministic local-fixture path (`--bronze-root`) already reads both Eurostat and World Bank via `silver.stats.load.frames_from_bronze`, and the headline real Gold (2,968x4, World Bank `rail_freight_tonne_km` + `rail_network_length_km`) was produced through that local path. But the live MinIO branch reads Eurostat TSVs only; World Bank JSON is never listed or parsed. Since World Bank is currently the only stats source that maps to a real Gold feature, a real live run yields a feature-less / empty Gold stats matrix, undermining the "live lakehouse" evidence claim for the report (Contract C in docs/TASKS.md).

**Problem.** In `src/railway_lakehouse/pipeline.py`, `_read_bronze_stats_frames(lander)` (lines 193-210) has two branches. The local branch (lines 200-202): `if getattr(lander, "bronze_root", None) is not None: return stats_load.frames_from_bronze(local_root)` correctly reads BOTH sources because `frames_from_bronze` iterates `_SOURCES = {"worldbank": ..., "eurostat": ...}` (src/railway_lakehouse/silver/stats/load.py:76-79, 87-111). The live/s3 branch (lines 204-209) only does `raw_eurostat_tables = _read_bronze_eurostat(lander)` then `read_eurostat_tsv(...)`; there is NO World Bank equivalent. `_read_bronze_eurostat` (pipeline.py:178-189) calls `_list_bronze_files(lander, domain="stats", source="eurostat", ...)` — World Bank objects under `stats/worldbank/...` are never globbed. Net effect: on a live MinIO run (`lander = RawLander()`, which has `.s3` but no `bronze_root`, lander.py:44-54), `_read_bronze_stats_frames` returns Eurostat-only frames; since no Eurostat label currently maps to a canonical feature in practice (the headline Gold feature came from World Bank), `merge_sources` drops everything and Gold is silently empty. There is also no warning when zero World Bank frames are found in the live branch, so the failure is silent. Existing tests cover only the local branch (tests/test_pipeline_gaps.py:38-48 `test_pipeline_stats_reader_loads_eurostat_and_worldbank_fixtures` injects `SimpleNamespace(bronze_root=...)`); the s3 branch of `_read_bronze_stats_frames` has zero coverage.

**Steps.**
1. Re-read the local-mode loaders to reuse them verbatim: `load_worldbank_frame(raw: bytes, dataset_id: str)` and `load_eurostat_frame(raw: bytes, dataset_id: str)` in src/railway_lakehouse/silver/stats/load.py:39-71. These already do all deterministic byte-level parsing (JSON melt, gzip-decompress, `source_system` tagging) and return the long contract `[geo, year, value, unit, source_dataset, source_column, source_system]`. The live branch should call these on s3-read bytes rather than re-implementing parsing.
2. In pipeline.py add a new private reader `_read_bronze_worldbank(lander) -> list[pd.DataFrame]` mirroring `_read_bronze_eurostat` (pipeline.py:178-189): call `_list_bronze_files(lander, domain="stats", source="worldbank", include=lambda name: name.endswith(".json"))`, derive `dataset_id = _dataset_id_from_path(path, "worldbank")`, read the raw bytes via the s3 filesystem, and pass them to `stats_load.load_worldbank_frame(raw_bytes, dataset_id)`. Skip catalogue datasets whose dataset_id starts with `_` (e.g. `_catalogue_*`) to mirror frames_from_bronze (load.py:97) so catalogue JSON is never fed to the WB loader. Append only non-empty frames.
3. Add a byte-reading helper for s3/local symmetry, e.g. `_read_bytes(lander, path) -> bytes`: `if isinstance(path, Path): return Path(path).read_bytes()` else `with lander.s3.open(path, "rb") as f: return f.read()`. (`_read_tsv` at pipeline.py:269-274 and `_read_text` at 277-281 already show the isinstance(Path) vs lander.s3.open pattern; reuse the same shape. Do NOT route through `_read_text` — World Bank bytes must be read as bytes so `load_worldbank_frame`'s gzip/JSON handling and encoding stay correct, and so this does not collide with GAP-014's text-encoding work.)
4. Rewrite the live branch of `_read_bronze_stats_frames` (pipeline.py:204-209) to read BOTH sources symmetrically. Keep the existing Eurostat reader (or refactor it to also go through `load_eurostat_frame` for parity — optional, note pitfall about dtype drift). Concatenate Eurostat frames + the new World Bank frames into the returned list. The local branch (lines 200-202) stays unchanged.
5. Add a deterministic WARNING when the live branch finds zero World Bank frames (closure criterion requires it): after collecting WB frames in the live branch, `if not worldbank_frames: log.warning("Live stats read found zero World Bank frames under stats/worldbank/*; live Gold stats matrix will be feature-less. Check MinIO Bronze landing.")`. Use the module logger `log` (pipeline.py:42).
6. Ensure the live Bronze LANDING side also lands World Bank, not just Eurostat: inspect pipeline.py:96-100 (the `else` live branch). Today it calls `eurostat.ingest(lander)` and `past_recordings.ingest(lander, ...)` only — World Bank is never landed live. Add a World Bank ingest call alongside `eurostat.ingest(lander)` using the existing Bronze World Bank source adapter. Confirm the adapter exists under src/railway_lakehouse/bronze/sources/ (the live_check path already collects `worldbank` per docs/GAP_REGISTER.md:111,119) and import + call its `ingest(lander)` the same way eurostat does. If the adapter's entry point differs from `ingest(lander)`, match its real signature — do not invent one.
7. Add a deterministic integration test in tests/test_pipeline_gaps.py (which is `pytestmark = pytest.mark.integration`, line 9) named e.g. `test_pipeline_live_stats_branch_reads_worldbank_via_fake_s3`. Build a tiny in-test fake `s3` object (a class or SimpleNamespace) exposing `.glob(pattern)` -> list of POSIX path strings and `.open(path, mode)` -> a context manager returning the fixture bytes ("rb") or text ("r"). Seed it from the committed fixtures: `tests/fixtures/bronze/stats/worldbank/IS.RRS.PASG.KM/ingest_date=2026-06-22/IS.RRS.PASG.KM.json` and `tests/fixtures/bronze/stats/eurostat/rail_passengers_demo/ingest_date=2026-06-22/passengers.tsv`, keyed under the `bronze/` bucket prefix so the glob pattern `bronze/stats/<source>/*/ingest_date=*/*` matches (see _list_bronze_files pattern at pipeline.py:259). Inject `lander = SimpleNamespace(s3=fake)` (NO `bronze_root`). Assert `_read_bronze_stats_frames(lander)` returns at least one frame with `source_system == 'worldbank'` AND at least one with `'eurostat'`.
8. Add a second assertion (or test) that the zero-WB warning fires: seed the fake s3 with only the Eurostat object, call `_read_bronze_stats_frames` under `caplog.at_level(logging.WARNING)`, and assert a warning mentioning World Bank was logged and no WB frame is returned.
9. Run the verification command and the full suite; update docs/GAP_REGISTER.md (set GAP-013 to a closed/in_progress state with evidence) and append a row to the Test Failure Mapping table. If a live MinIO run is performed, record the resulting Gold counts.json under output/evidence/ (do not commit large raw Bronze).

**Files to touch:** `C:\Users\XxX360QUICKSCOPERXxX\Documents\tmp\ai-masters\coursework\bigdata\course_proj\src\railway_lakehouse\pipeline.py`  `C:\Users\XxX360QUICKSCOPERXxX\Documents\tmp\ai-masters\coursework\bigdata\course_proj\tests\test_pipeline_gaps.py`  `C:\Users\XxX360QUICKSCOPERXxX\Documents\tmp\ai-masters\coursework\bigdata\course_proj\docs\GAP_REGISTER.md`

**Definition of Done (contract).**
